Selected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon
423
Compiled by the Editorial Committee of Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Speeches

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Kook Jin Hwan
Rev. Sun Myung Moon, who at the age of 16 received a calling from Heaven for the salvation of humanity, lived his entire life centered on the Heavenly Way with a single-minded devotion. He described his life as follows:
"If Rev. Moon has any assets, it is the suffering I endured for the public rather than for myself; that is my only asset. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I also tried to suffer more than anyone else. ... Until now, I have faced countless opposition and persecution from nations and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. There has never been a time in history when the world united to eliminate one person as they did with me. In that sense, I am a world champion. However, despite being cursed, I did not perish or collapse. I emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. ... Rev. Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Selected Speeches, Vol. 105, pp. 101-103)
Rev. Moon's life can be summed up in one word: 'suffering.' This suffering was not for himself but for God and humanity. From this, we come to understand who he is. He is the Messiah and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years, and he has come as the True Parent of humanity. Already, in 185 countries around the world, disciples following him are realizing the ideal of True Families with this faith confession.
Rev. Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history and the world, and the spirit world are clarified through his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, more importantly, his words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through his words. Although the level of his words is too high and deep to fully comprehend, they fundamentally have three characteristics.
First, through his words and life, he revealed God. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the bloodline of evil, they are children but cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. The sorrowful God, who was tragically alienated due to human sin, was made to 'speak' by Rev. Moon. He liberated God, who was silenced and trapped in church authority, doctrine, and ornate buildings, and made Him 'speak.' He made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' making Rev. Moon the 'perfect revelation of God.'
Secondly, he liberated humanity from ignorance and confusion. Although humans have reasoning and can make value judgments, they cannot fully explain their own existence, which is a tragic reality. Furthermore, humans are not independent beings but interdependent beings inseparable from others, yet they could not explain this relationship. This is because they lost God's words. Rev. Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Moreover, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete exemplary path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, he liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God possesses unique value as an individual truth body. Although this value should be fully realized under the dominion of original human beings, it has not been, causing all things to lament. Through his words, Rev. Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things and opened the way for their liberation by restoring humans to their original form.
Rev. and Mrs. Moon, who have come as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly deliver speeches worldwide, demonstrating through their substantial lives the teachings of 'using the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'living for the sake of others,' and striving to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Furthermore, through his words of life, noble life, and achievements, Rev. Moon has finally restored God's sovereignty and settled as the King of Blessed Families on earth as we enter the new millennium. He has been acclaimed as the King of Peace by peace activists from various fields, centered on politics and religion worldwide. He has also founded the Abel UN, the Universal Peace Federation, to realize a new world peace by breaking down the barriers of nations, races, and religions, and is working tirelessly to realize the ideal of a borderless, peaceful human family in 185 countries worldwide.
I hope that readers who encounter these words will establish a true value system for life that humanity must follow, form true families, and become key players in realizing a true world of peace in the new millennium as owners of Cheon Il Guk. *

That God is not the God of any country. He is my God. Say it. My God! "My God!" Humans themselves should have called Him Father, but they have never called Him Father. They have never called Him Mother.

When your mind commands your body, when you try to do something bad, whether day or night, 24 hours, whenever you try to do that action, it puts on the brakes. Without a country, marriage registration and birth registration cannot be done
The original nature of love is absolute, unique, unchanging, and eternal. The main attribute of God

The Four Mainstream Attributes of Love

Even if they want to eat it, they fight to chew on the flat dried squid. That's why they can't digest it. They can't digest President Moon. They get sick. So they have to vomit it out, cleanse it, and become clean to have a way to live.

The Hoon Dok meeting is to peel that off. The housewives should become the kings of the Hoon Dok meeting. You should evangelize ten times, a hundred times more diligently than the established churches. Jesus also said to forgive sinners seventy times seven times, so you must work harder than that. Otherwise, you'll fall out. You must know that the final fruit of women's suffering is offered at the Unification Church, and only by offering that fruit can your family women be liberated.

Do you understand, woman like a man? "Yes." Try doing it like this here. If you do this and cut the tail here, you don't look like a man, do you? Then put a hairpin here, and do what the children do. That's fine. It makes you look younger and more feminine. Wear earrings too. The earrings are small. Wear a necklace and rings, and wear women's shoes. If you wear flat shoes, people think you're a man and women run away. When you walk with a female friend. Do it like that. Do you understand? "Yes." Your voice is a woman's voice again. Will you do it or not? Will you do it or not? "I will." I thought it would be a man's voice then, but you're still a woman, even if I curse. Do well. Now!

(Hoon Dok reading from the Cheon Seong Gyeong, 'True Parents' section, 'The Necessity of True Parents')

The person who makes you the master of love
'1) The Need for Universal Parents
Originally, God created Adam and Eve, hoping that both could be perfected by having the fruit of children as parents and children having the fruit of parents.'

Yes. It's not the mother who makes the mother have a mother's love. When a bloody baby cries out with a high-pitched voice, at that time, whether it's a son or a daughter, the chest boils over as bone of bones and flesh of flesh. Have you all felt that or not? Even if you hate your husband, you can't hate your son. You must not hate future generations. Do you understand? "Yes."

In the past, it's okay to hate the archangel. Since the son is blessed and born as God's son and daughter, you must feel true love, not as an enemy for generations, but to bless them. Feeling God's heart, God was happier than us when He created Adam and Eve, feeling more joy than that, wherever you go, whether eating or sleeping, you first think of the baby.

Women have a lot of potential to do that, right? "Yes." In America, women go around playing, having chained their babies to the bed. These rascals! When they come back, the babies have pooped and are crying. There are cases where they fell and died. Seeing that, I thought I should get rid of these women with no sense. I hope there are no such women here in Yeosu and Suncheon. Do you hope there aren't any, or do you hope there are? "We hope there aren't any." You know, don't you? (Laughter) Now!

'...The reason parents are needed is to conquer the Heavenly Kingdom, and the reason parents want their children's love is to conquer the earth. The parent's heart is the heart of heaven. When do you know this heart of heaven? You don't know it as a child. You know it only when you become a parent.'

The child lets you know. It's not the parents who make the parents the masters of love. The child decides the master of love. By loving the wife, the husband can conquer the half-woman. Who does that? It's the husband who makes the woman the master of love, and it's the woman who makes the husband the master of love. You didn't know that.

If you make a brother, the brother stands in the position of God's love, so by having a younger sibling, you can love like a father and mother, so the brotherly love that is equal to God's love is established. Love is all the same. Even if you live in the same house, there is no complaint. Because you live for each other, you become one. Without having such a theoretical family foundation, you can't have a peaceful kingdom. You must know that no third-party cunning content can intervene. Do you understand or not? "Yes!"

If you educate the wives, the husbands will have to treat the teacher to a bulgogi feast every day, but they did all sorts of things to kill him. Men are fundamentally supposed to serve women, children, and the family.

The church is unnecessary. If you become God's family, the church is unnecessary. Now is the era of dismantling the church and the state. It's a world where the extended family and clan ideology centered on God is expanded. Heaven and earth become like that. You can't freely go back and forth between the boundary lines of hell and heaven. If you abolish the boundary lines, you can freely go back and forth.

God's sons and daughters' families are the resting place of unification, the base of peace
Here, as I said earlier, even if you go to the remote areas of Africa, you must cross the border at once without hesitation. By changing the extremes, you cross hundreds or thousands of boundary lines in between. So in the Unification Church, marrying a white person and a black person is not a problem. Marrying an African person, the difference between the rich and poor in the South and North is not a problem. Since they are brothers, it's natural to sell property to marry off a younger brother or sister.

The tradition of God's sons and daughters' families is so strong that it becomes the resting place of unification. Then it becomes the base of peace. You must know that it's not even a problem! You have to say 'Amen.' "Amen!" Say Amen. "Amen!" Amen means 'Ah, admirable man and woman!' Amen means you are number one. The number one man is God's son and daughter.

What does Amen mean? It means 'Let it be as you wish!' Who wishes? It's not President Moon, but God. It's not to make a woman President Moon wants, but to make a woman God wants. After making a great husband and a great sister, waiting for the brother to come, teaching the son with tear marks, you must know that a new race is born. You can't have a family that makes the children cry by fighting like a stray dog and divorcing.

Even parents are like that. There are many sons and daughters, but when they come to greet the parents in the morning, you know who is coming by the footsteps. No matter how much you cry, stop! 'Number 13!' Then it must stop. Then you wipe your tears. No matter how much you cry, when you come like this, you kiss and teach them to kiss the father. That's the way to make a filial child in the family. Do you understand, women? "Yes."

From now on, you must do so. Even if your husband looks like a squid... Do you know squid? There must be squid here. You know squid, right? "Yes." It's a miserable thing that was struck by lightning and lives in a hole in the ground, not becoming an octopus or a cuttlefish. It was supposed to become a cuttlefish but became a squid. Even if you put a squid in your mouth, it can't bite, right? An octopus bites, right? If a cuttlefish wraps around you, it can kill a person. It has the power to win.

God's sons and daughters have become squid. The person who should have been the wife of the Creator who made the octopus became the wife of a squid's offspring, can you find that? You must clean the room so that God can come without any deficiency, making a holy altar, so that the governor can visit, the president of the country can visit, and through the president's introduction, God can come.

You must become the family of filial children of the eight provinces, then the family of loyal subjects, so that the president visits and can graft onto the heavenly kingdom, then Korea can graft onto the country of world saints. Women must liberate the country. You rascal girls! Who caused God to lose the country? Isn't it women? Women ruined heaven and earth. Now I am putting women forward to make them the elder sisters of the royal family of heaven, not the pitiful kings of hell, to make them mothers, grandmothers, and kings.

The king of kings becomes the cosmic parent, the cosmic earth parent, the cosmic earth human parent, and without having a family that can guide heaven and earth, God's liberation, the liberation of the cosmic earth parent, and the liberation of the cosmic earth human parent cannot be achieved. The purpose of the teacher is to create a cosmic earth family that can go to heaven for your descendants. You must know that the teacher is creating a family model. Do you understand or not? "Yes!" Listen well. Now!

Repent your past and get the certificate of a national representative
'The work of conquering the two worlds and making them one is love. When this happens, the parent-child relationship is a glorious parent-child relationship. It's the same. You can't turn anyone back, and you can't turn anyone forward. It's one. At that time, it is called a glorious parent-child relationship.

So people say that those without parents are pitiful. Why? They have no way to conquer the spiritual and physical worlds. They also say that those without children are pitiful.'

They are orphans and widows. Widowers! They can't conquer the spiritual world. When you marry with first love, you must make everything at that time to go to heaven even if you die. If you don't receive a welcome from the entire family within 3 to 4 years of first love, you can't become a mother who inherits the royal authority of that family. You must know that a mother must raise a filial child, and a husband must raise a loyal subject, nurturing and feeding the mother and children with the loyal subject's rice, following the public official's rules, and growing with the public official's salary.

Therefore, wherever the husband goes, the wife and child automatically follow. If you become the president of the world, even if you have enemies like the Communist Party, and criminals in prison, if you are the president's children, you can live in the president's house, right? You don't know how precious it is to receive the love of parents. For that, you must repent all your past and have even a fake certificate of a national representative. Do you understand? "Yes."

You too. Even if you became all sorts of evil in front of the teacher, you must have a fake certificate of the association president, a certificate of a national representative. Only then can the representative of that country's sovereignty, land, and people say, 'This is the person who can lead to heaven among them. Isn't he the elder brother? If you love from the position of a younger brother, you will be saved.' When you say this to God, He can't say no. 'Really? Try it.' That's why you must love and embrace the church members more than your siblings.

A mother must raise a filial child, and a father must raise a loyal subject
Everything you've lived so far has been a lie. You didn't know what the Hoon Dok meeting was, and the words just flowed by. It's not yours. Only by sharing it can the royal authority of the peaceful world, wherever you go, whether to the northern end, the southern end, the western end, or the eastern end, 360 degrees, go to the center without any problem. So you must liberate. If you liberate, you must liberate the country and make even all things serve the owner. You must release them. Liberation is easy.

After World War II, the Korean people were liberated, but you must release all things. Since the position of the owner who created all things was lost, all things are groaning. Isn't it written in Romans 8? It says all things are groaning, right? "Yes." They cry out, 'Abba Father.' It's to receive the name of an adopted son. They can't go to the position of a son.

So, since all things were sacrificed and groaned due to the fall, women must focus on that work, creating filial children in the family, and the mother must open the path of loyalty that the husband will take. If the beloved child kisses the mother, the mother must go and kiss, and the mother must kiss the husband so that the child thinks, 'This is the mouth my mom loves,' and kisses the dad. Do you know that becomes the tradition of the family? Western people kiss when they meet. It's that tradition. If you kiss with an evil temptation, a fox's kiss, it becomes a ruinous seed.

The mother must teach. A mother must raise a filial child, and a father must raise a loyal subject. The mother of a loyal subject must raise a loyal subject's son with the bloodline of a loyal subject, in the standard of being one body, and establish the tradition that she is undoubtedly the counterpart of a loyal subject before the father. But what is divorce? In a trial, they fight to take the children. In a country like America, if they don't give anything to the women in a trial, (divorce) will decrease by more than half. I am trying to immediately amend the law to liberate women.

In such a world, women put on makeup and become fake women. Do you know that an eighty-year-old woman can become an elementary school student with makeup skills? Do you know that in the acting world? It's no problem for a sixty-year-old woman to become an elementary, middle, or high school student. So who do you trust? How do you distinguish? Women over sixty become street women looking like twenty-year-old maidens. When you find out, oh my, when you try to marry, you find out she is of grandmother age.

That's the world now. There's nothing to trust in that world. You can't even trust President Moon. He might betray someday. Even if President Moon betrays his substitutes, you must have the resolve to become the kingpin in liberating God, and not become a minus condition, and think that even if President Moon abandons the Unification Church, you will establish it, to become a son or daughter who can be embraced by God! Amen. "Amen!" I am not telling you to be embraced by President Moon. So I am not a fake teacher. I am real. Is that right or not? "It's right." Listen well. Read! (Hoon Dok reading until the end of Chapter 3, followed by a prayer by President Moon Pyung-rae)

As sons and daughters of the Parents, become Hoon Dok teachers who rule over all nations
Now, after breakfast, is it the evening of farewell or the morning? "It's morning." (Bow)

What kind of people are the Japanese? Raise your hand. "Raise your hand if you are married from Japan." There are many! *You are not Japanese women. You must clearly know that as daughters of God, you must transcend the nation. Do you understand? "Yes." No matter how hard it is, you must not think of Japan. You must not forget the fact that you came to marry to abolish that national border. Do you understand? "Yes." If there are Western women, raise your hand! There are none! (*The following is spoken in Japanese)

Are there no Westerners? "There are no Westerners." Then it will be easy. If there were, it would be difficult. In Seoul, you don't know how many Westerners there are. How complicated it would be to make them all one?

Korea and Japan are like cousins. So you must become one, and Korean people must not look down on Japanese people. Do you understand? "Yes." You must love them like younger siblings. They were born wrong. Since the younger sibling was raised by a nanny and didn't know the parents, you must awaken to the responsibility of raising them well so they can serve the parents well, and become a model of unity. Do you understand? "Yes." Do well.

Now, since you came here, eat as if you are eating at your brother's house, your sister's house, your uncle's house, or your parents' house. Even if the side dishes are not tasty, since you have eaten sea bass and all the fish of the sea, you will like it if you buy pork and beef and eat it. Did you buy such things? "We prepared rice cake soup for breakfast." Rice cake soup must have beef in it. "Yes."

So eat deliciously like the delicacies of the mountains and seas, gain strength, and since the teacher has become an old grandfather, you must think, 'I am the son and daughter of the young teacher who can rule over all nations, my children, my family!' With such a heart, you must work hard and become Hoon Dok teachers! Amen! "Amen!" Applause! (Applause)

"Please come to Yeosu again!" Come again? Let me die, and then tell me to come again? (Laughter) If you say come again, there's a possibility I won't come. If you say, "Please come to Yeosu," it's good because I can come. Try saying, "Please come to Yeosu!" "Please come to Yeosu!" I'll come! (Laughter. Applause) *
